Product Description

   We offer you 10 Pieces of Alex Grey’s Hofmann LSD Blotter.

   On the front you see a very detailed drawing A. Hofmann with his
   extraordinary formula.
   Those famous Blotter are dosed very professionally and each Piece is
   contains about 100-125ug of LSD.
   The effects are very constantly and energetic providing positive
   feelings and a constant Trip.

   Alex Grey Blotter a highest grade of clean LSD,
   energetic, light visual awesome Quality (so called needlepoint LSD).
   Highest Grade of Purity I have ever seen.
   No taste, pure and smooth effects, Just LSD.

   Very clear trip very suitable for Beginners.
   Friendly and shiny with light clear effects on the mind.
   Go and get them. You will have gentle vibes of high Quality Acid maybe
   with some drinks ;-)…

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

   Beginners:
   Take a half or full one for the Start Up.

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

Product Description

   We offer you 25 Pieces of Alex Grey’s Hofmann LSD Blotter.

   On the front you see a very detailed drawing A. Hofmann with his
   extraordinary formula.
   Those famous Blotter are dosed very professionally and each Piece is
   contains about 100-125ug of LSD.
   The effects are very constantly and energetic providing positive
   feelings and a constant Trip.

   Alex Grey Blotter a highest grade of clean LSD,
   energetic, light visual awesome Quality (so called needlepoint LSD).
   Highest Grade of Purity I have ever seen.
   No taste, pure and smooth effects, Just LSD.

   Very clear trip very suitable for Beginners.
   Friendly and shiny with light clear effects on the mind.
   Go and get them. You will have gentle vibes of high Quality Acid maybe
   with some drinks ;-)…

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

   Beginners:
   Take a half or full one for the Start Up.

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

Product Description

Product Description

   We offer you 200 Pieces of Alex Grey’s Hofmann LSD Blotter.

   On the front you see a very detailed drawing A. Hofmann with his
   extraordinary formula.
   Those famous Blotter are dosed very professionally and each Piece is
   contains about 100-125ug of LSD.
   The effects are very constantly and energetic providing positive
   feelings and a constant Trip.

   Alex Grey Blotter a highest grade of clean LSD,
   energetic, light visual awesome Quality (so called needlepoint LSD).
   Highest Grade of Purity I have ever seen.
   No taste, pure and smooth effects, Just LSD.

   Very clear trip very suitable for Beginners.
   Friendly and shiny with light clear effects on the mind.
   Go and get them. You will have gentle vibes of high Quality Acid maybe
   with some drinks ;-)…

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

   Beginners:
   Take a half or full one for the Start Up.

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

Product Description

   We offer you 25 Pieces of Koi LSD Blotter.

   Those beautiful and absolutely tasteless Blotter are dosed with white
   LSD Crystals.
   Each Piece contains about 100-125ug of LSD.

   The effects are shiny and gentle.

Product Description

   We offer you 10 Pieces of Koi LSD Blotter.

   Those beautiful and absolutely tasteless Blotter are dosed with white
   LSD Crystals.
   Each Piece contains about 100-125ug of LSD.

   The effects are shiny and gentle.
   This Acid is very colorful like the drawing.

   White Fluff Crystals are clean and Shiny like a rainbow.

   Koi Fish is a symbol for Luck and Fortune.
   Those Blotter are definitely a good choice for Beginners.
   Smooth vibes and very friendly.

Product Description

   You get 10x selflaid LSD Eric Snowden Blotters.
   The blotters are laid with 100ug needlepoint crystal (purity 98%+), so
   get ready for a nice pure and clean trip!
   These blotters are more for beginners, experienced users should try our
   “Shiva” blotters, which are laid with 200ug of our crystal!

Info

   Ordering

   Please provide your correct shipping address to make sure that you will
   receive your order.

   Payment goes only in bitcoin, please don’t ask for alternatives.


   Refund & Reshipping

   We will not reship or refund anything if you have provided a wrong
   shipping address.

   If you haven’t received your order after 3-4 weeks, please contact us
   and we will reship 50% or refund 20%.


   Shipping

   Shipping is free, and takes 1-2 weeks, depending on where you live.

   We use a stealth shipping method to ship the products world wide.

Product Description

   We offer you 100 Pieces of Alex Grey’s Hofmann LSD Blotter.

   On the front you see a very detailed drawing A. Hofmann with his
   extraordinary formula.
   Those famous Blotter are dosed very professionally and each Piece is
   contains about 100-125ug of LSD.
   The effects are very constantly and energetic providing positive
   feelings and a constant Trip.

   Alex Grey Blotter a highest grade of clean LSD,
   energetic, light visual awesome Quality (so called needlepoint LSD).
   Highest Grade of Purity I have ever seen.
   No taste, pure and smooth effects, Just LSD.

   Very clear trip very suitable for Beginners.
   Friendly and shiny with light clear effects on the mind.
   Go and get them. You will have gentle vibes of high Quality Acid maybe
   with some drinks ;-)…

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

   Beginners:
   Take a half or full one for the Start Up.

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

Info

   Ordering

   Please provide your correct shipping address to make sure that you will
   receive your order.

   Payment goes only in bitcoin, please don’t ask for alternatives.


   Refund & Reshipping

   We will not reship or refund anything if you have provided a wrong
   shipping address.

   If you haven’t received your order after 3-4 weeks, please contact us
   and we will reship 50% or refund 20%.


   Shipping

   Shipping is free, and takes 1-2 weeks, depending on where you live.

   We use a stealth shipping method to ship the products world wide.

Product Description

   You get 25x selflaid LSD Eric Snowden Blotters.
   The blotters are laid with 100ug needlepoint crystal (purity 98%+), so
   get ready for a nice pure and clean trip!
   These blotters are more for beginners, experienced users should try our
   “Shiva” blotters, which are laid with 200ug of our crystal!

Product Description

   You get 5x selflaid LSD Eric Snowden Blotters.
   The blotters are laid with 100ug needlepoint crystal (purity 98%+), so
   get ready for a nice pure and clean trip!
   These blotters are more for beginners, experienced users should try our
   “Shiva” blotters, which are laid with 200ug of our crystal!

Product Description

   We offer you 50 Pieces of Alex Grey’s Hofmann LSD Blotter.

   On the front you see a very detailed drawing A. Hofmann with his
   extraordinary formula.
   Those famous Blotter are dosed very professionally and each Piece is
   contains about 100-125ug of LSD.
   The effects are very constantly and energetic providing positive
   feelings and a constant Trip.

   Alex Grey Blotter a highest grade of clean LSD,
   energetic, light visual awesome Quality (so called needlepoint LSD).
   Highest Grade of Purity I have ever seen.
   No taste, pure and smooth effects, Just LSD.

   Very clear trip very suitable for Beginners.
   Friendly and shiny with light clear effects on the mind.
   Go and get them. You will have gentle vibes of high Quality Acid maybe
   with some drinks ;-)…

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

   Beginners:
   Take a half or full one for the Start Up.

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

Product Description

   We offer you 100 Pieces of Alex Grey’s Hofmann LSD Blotter.

   On the front you see a very detailed drawing A. Hofmann with his
   extraordinary formula.
   Those famous Blotter are dosed very professionally and each Piece is
   contains about 100-125ug of LSD.
   The effects are very constantly and energetic providing positive
   feelings and a constant Trip.

   Alex Grey Blotter a highest grade of clean LSD,
   energetic, light visual awesome Quality (so called needlepoint LSD).
   Highest Grade of Purity I have ever seen.
   No taste, pure and smooth effects, Just LSD.

   Very clear trip very suitable for Beginners.
   Friendly and shiny with light clear effects on the mind.
   Go and get them. You will have gentle vibes of high Quality Acid maybe
   with some drinks ;-)…

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

   Beginners:
   Take a half or full one for the Start Up.

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

Product Description

   We offer you 10 Pieces of Alex Grey’s Hofmann LSD Blotter.

   On the front you see a very detailed drawing A. Hofmann with his
   extraordinary formula.
   Those famous Blotter are dosed very professionally and each Piece is
   contains about 100-125ug of LSD.
   The effects are very constantly and energetic providing positive
   feelings and a constant Trip.

   Alex Grey Blotter a highest grade of clean LSD,
   energetic, light visual awesome Quality (so called needlepoint LSD).
   Highest Grade of Purity I have ever seen.
   No taste, pure and smooth effects, Just LSD.

   Very clear trip very suitable for Beginners.
   Friendly and shiny with light clear effects on the mind.
   Go and get them. You will have gentle vibes of high Quality Acid maybe
   with some drinks ;-)…

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.

   Beginners:
   Take a half or full one for the Start Up.

   Easy to handle Acid with a friendly dose of 100-125ug of pure LSD.
